--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
    /**
     * 读取 SharedPreferences 中上次保存的 accent hex，将主题色同步注入启动画面视图。
     * 首次安装或未存储时使用默认紫色（与 Web 端初始主题一致）。
     * 应在 setContentView 之后、WebView 加载之前调用。
     */
    private fun applySavedAccentToSplash() {
        val hex = getSharedPreferences("gm_prefs", MODE_PRIVATE)
            .getString("accent_hex", "#8B4CF8") ?: "#8B4CF8"
        try {
            val color = Color.parseColor(hex)
            val tintList = android.content.res.ColorStateList.valueOf(color)

            // 进度条
            splashOverlay.findViewById<android.widget.ProgressBar>(R.id.splashProgress)
                ?.let { pb ->
                    pb.indeterminateTintList = tintList
                    pb.progressTintList      = tintList
                }

            // 光标块
            splashOverlay.findViewById<View>(R.id.splashCursor)
                ?.setBackgroundColor(color)

            // 终端提示符 $
            splashOverlay.findViewById<android.widget.TextView>(R.id.splashPrompt)
                ?.setTextColor(color)

            // 浅色模式下 Octocat 图标跟随 accent 色；深色模式保持白色
            val nightMask = resources.configuration.uiMode and
                android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_MASK
            val isNight = nightMask == android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_YES
            if (!isNight) {
                splashOverlay.findViewById<android.widget.ImageView>(R.id.splashLogo)
                    ?.imageTintList = tintList
            }

            // 四角装饰线：统一注入 accent 色（带透明度）
            val cornerAlpha = 0x40  // 25% 透明度
            val cornerColor = (cornerAlpha shl 24) or (color and 0x00FFFFFF)
            listOf(
                R.id.splashCornerTL, R.id.splashCornerTR,
                R.id.splashCornerBL, R.id.splashCornerBR
            ).forEach { id ->
                splashOverlay.findViewById<android.view.ViewGroup>(id)?.let { group ->
                    for (i in 0 until group.childCount) {
                        group.getChildAt(i).setBackgroundColor(cornerColor)
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (_: Exception) { /* 非法 hex，使用 XML 默认色，静默忽略 */ }
    }

    // ── 生命周期 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {

<resources>
    <!-- 启动图标背景：紫色（与 Web 端主题色一致） -->
    <color name="ic_launcher_background">#7c3aed</color>

    <!-- 底部导航栏颜色 -->

      ══ 启动画面 · 浅色模式配色 ══
      GitHub Light 风格：干净白底 + 紫色点缀

Before API 29, using `%p` in gradient radius would cause an `InflateException` at runtime, which would crash the app immediately on launch!\n\nHowever, `minSdk = 26` (Android 8.0), so devices running Android 8.0, 8.1, and 9.0 (API 26-28) would crash on launch because they can\'t parse `55%p`.\n\nActually wait - let me double check. In some contexts it may also be relative to the parent dimensions (followed by `%p`).\n\nThe `%p` (percentage of parent) was available from API 1 for dimension attributes, but for `gradientRadius` in `GradientDrawable`, the `%p` suffix support might have been added later.\n\nActually, checking more carefully: The `gradientRadius` attribute accepts dimension values including `%p` (parent-relative) in drawable XMLs.     private fun handleExitOnBack() {
        if (backPressedOnce) {
            // 第二次按下：退出应用
            backHandler.removeCallbacksAndMessages(null)
            finish()
            return
        }
        backPressedOnce = true
        Toast.makeText(this, "再按一次退出应用", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        // 2 秒后重置标志
        backHandler.postDelayed({ backPressedOnce = false }, 2000)
    }

    // ── WebView 配置 ────────────────────────────────────────────────

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    private fun setupWebViewSettings() {
        // WebView 背景跟随当前主题，避免深色/浅色主题下背景颜色不一致
        val bgHex = if (darkTheme) "#111117" else "#f8f8fb"
        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor(bgHex))
        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true
            allowContentAccess = true
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }
    }

    private fun setupWebViewClient() {
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false

                // 本地资源：让 WebView 自己处理
                if (url.startsWith("file://")) return false

                // 外部链接（http/https）：一律用系统浏览器打开，避免破坏 React 应用历史栈。
                // 若允许 WebView 加载外部页面，React Router 的 history.state.idx
                // 会丢失，返回键无法回到应用内部路由。
                if (url.startsWith("https://") || url.startsWith("http://")) {
                    runCatching {
                        val intent = Intent(Intent.ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(url))
                        startActivity(intent)
                    }
                    return true // 阻止 WebView 自行加载
                }

                // 其他协议（tel:、mailto: 等）：交系统处理
                return true
            }

            /**
             * 每次页面导航完成后，从 URL fragment（HashRouter）中解析当前路径，
             * 并同步更新底部导航栏的选中状态。
             * 例如：file:///android_asset/index.html#/repos/owner/name → path = "/repos/..."
             */
            override fun onPageFinished(view: WebView?, url: String?) {
                super.onPageFinished(view, url)
                val hash = url?.substringAfter("#", "") ?: return
                val path = if (hash.startsWith("/")) hash else "/$hash"
                syncBottomNavSelection(path)

                // 首次加载完成后从 localStorage 读取主题并同步原生颜色
                // github_manager_theme 是 ThemeContext 使用的 key
                view?.evaluateJavascript(
                    "(function(){ return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_theme') || 'dark'; })()"
                ) { result ->
                    val raw = result?.trim('"') ?: "system"
                    // 持久化最新主题设置，供下次冷启动恢复
                    getSharedPreferences("gm_prefs", MODE_PRIVATE)
                        .edit().putString("theme_mode", raw).apply()
                    val resolved = when (raw) {
                        "light" -> false
                        "dark"  -> true
                        else    -> { // system
                            val nightMode = resources.configuration.uiMode and
                                android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_MASK
                            nightMode == android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_YES
                        }
                    }
                    runOnUiThread { applyNativeTheme(resolved) }

                    // 同时读取强调色方案，将选中色同步为存储的 previewColor
                    val accentMap = mapOf(
                        "purple" to "#8B4CF8",
                        "blue"   to "#1d6be3",
                        "green"  to "#16a34a",
                        "orange" to "#f97316",
                        "rose"   to "#e11d48",
                        "cyan"   to "#0891b2",
                    )
                    view?.evaluateJavascript(
                        "(function(){ return localStorage.getItem('github_manager_accent') || 'purple'; })()"
                    ) { accentResult ->
                        val accentId = accentResult?.trim('"') ?: "purple"
                        val hex = accentMap[accentId] ?: "#8B4CF8"
                        try {
                            val color = Color.parseColor(hex)
                            val isDark = darkTheme
                            val unselected = if (isDark) 0xFF9292A8.toInt() else 0xFF64748B.toInt()
                            val iconColors = android.content.res.ColorStateList(
                                arrayOf(intArrayOf(android.R.attr.state_checked), intArrayOf()),
                                intArrayOf(color, unselected)
                            )
                            runOnUiThread {
                                currentAccentColor = color
                                bottomNav.itemIconTintList = iconColors
                                bottomNav.itemTextColor   = iconColors
                            }
                        } catch (_: Exception) { /* 静默忽略 */ }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 根据当前路径前缀匹配导航菜单项，并更新 BottomNavigationView 选中状态。
     * 采用静默更新方式（禁用监听器 → 修改选中项 → 恢复监听器），避免触发重复导航。
     */
    private fun syncBottomNavSelection(path: String) {
        val targetId = navPathMap.entries.firstOrNull { (prefix, _) ->
            if (prefix == "/") path == "/" else path.startsWith(prefix)
        }?.value ?: R.id.nav_home

        if (targetId == currentNavItemId) return
        currentNavItemId = targetId

        // 静默更新：临时移除监听器，防止 setSelectedItemId 触发重复路由跳转
        bottomNav.setOnItemSelectedListener(null)
        bottomNav.selectedItemId = targetId
        setupBottomNavListener()
    }

    /**
     * 初始化底部导航栏：绑定点击监听，通过 evaluateJavascript 修改 HashRouter location。
     * 仅在目标 Tab 与当前页面不同时才执行导航，避免重刷当前页。
     */
    private fun setupBottomNav() {
        bottomNav.selectedItemId = R.id.nav_home
        setupBottomNavListener()
    }

    private fun setupBottomNavListener() {
        bottomNav.setOnItemSelectedListener { item ->
            val path = navPathMap.entries.firstOrNull { it.value == item.itemId }?.key ?: "/"
            val targetId = item.itemId
            if (targetId == currentNavItemId) return@setOnItemSelectedListener false

            // 通过修改 location.hash 触发 HashRouter 路由跳转
            val safeHash = path.replace("'", "\\'")
            webView.evaluateJavascript(
                "(function(){ window.location.hash = '$safeHash'; })()", null
            )
            true
        }
    }

    /**
     * 根据 Web 端传来的主题信号，同步更新原生系统 UI 颜色：
     *  - 状态栏背景色 & 图标颜色（深色主题用浅色图标，浅色主题用深色图标）
     *  - 系统导航栏（手势条/按键条）背景色
     *  - 底部导航栏背景色及图标/文字颜色
     *
     * 颜色值与 Web 端 index.css 的 HSL 变量保持一致：
     *   深色：background=#111117，sidebar-background=#0d0d11
     *   浅色：background=#f8f8fb，sidebar-background=#f6f4fa
     */
    private fun applyNativeTheme(isDark: Boolean) {
        darkTheme = isDark
        // 同步 WebView 背景色，避免白/黑背景闪烁
        webView.setBackgroundColor(
            Color.parseColor(if (isDark) "#111117" else "#f8f8fb")
        )
        if (isDark) {
            // ── 深色模式 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
            val bgColor      = Color.parseColor("#111117")  // --background dark
            val navBgColor   = Color.parseColor("#0d0d11")  // --sidebar-background dark
            val unselectedColor = Color.parseColor("#9292A8")  // --muted-foreground dark

            window.statusBarColor     = bgColor
            window.navigationBarColor = navBgColor
            bottomNav.setBackgroundColor(navBgColor)

            // 状态栏图标 → 浅色（白色）
            if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.R) {
                window.insetsController?.setSystemBarsAppearance(
                    0,
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS or
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS
                )
            } else {
                @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
                window.decorView.systemUiVisibility = window.decorView.systemUiVisibility and
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_STATUS_BAR.inv() and
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BAR.inv()
            }

            // 底部导航栏图标与文字颜色（选中色跟随当前强调色方案）
            val iconColors = android.content.res.ColorStateList(
                arrayOf(intArrayOf(android.R.attr.state_checked), intArrayOf()),
                intArrayOf(currentAccentColor, unselectedColor)
            )
            bottomNav.itemIconTintList = iconColors
            bottomNav.itemTextColor   = iconColors

        } else {
            // ── 浅色模式 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
            val bgColor      = Color.parseColor("#f8f8fb")  // --background light
            val navBgColor   = Color.parseColor("#f6f4fa")  // --sidebar-background light
            val unselectedColor = Color.parseColor("#64748b")  // 深灰，在浅色背景上可读

            window.statusBarColor     = bgColor
[The command completed with exit code 0.]

Using `Theme.MaterialComponents.Light.NoActionBar` should be fine.\n\n5. **IMPORTANT FINDING**: The theme style `android:windowBackground` is set to `@android:color/transparent`. But at the time `setupWebViewSettings()` is called:\n1. `setContentView()` is called\n2. `applySavedAccentToSplash()` is called\n3. `startSplashTypingAnimation()` is called\n4. `setupWebViewSettings()` is called\n\nThe `darkTheme` variable is only updated in `applyNativeTheme()` or `notifyTheme()` callback, which comes AFTER the WebView loads. The initial value is `true` (dark). This means the WebView background is always initially dark, even on light theme systems. This could cause a visual flash but not a crash.\n\n7. **Wait, I just realized something critical about `darkTheme`**: The initial value is `true`. But in `onCreate()`, the code determines `isInitialDark` based on the saved theme, but it NEVER sets `darkTheme` to match! So `darkTheme` remains `true` even if the device is in light mode. This means `setupWebViewSettings()` uses `darkTheme = true` (wrong for light mode).\n\nBut again, this causes visual issues, not crashes.\n\n8. **THE REAL CRASH**: Looking at the `onDestroy()`:\n```kotlin\noverride fun onDestroy() {\n    super.onDestroy()\n    splashHandler.removeCallbacksAndMessages(null)\n    unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)  // ← CRASH if not registered!\n    webView.stopLoading()\n    webView.destroy()\n}\n```\n\nIf ANY exception occurs before `registerDownloadReceiver()` in `onCreate()`, then:\n1. The Activity crashes in `onCreate()`\n2. `onDestroy()` is called\n3. `unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)` throws `IllegalArgumentException: Receiver not registered`\n4. This second exception crashes the process again\n\nThis creates a situation where the app appears to "immediately crash" from the user\'s perspective.\n\nBUT what causes the first crash? But domStorage IS enabled.\n\n**CRITICAL INSIGHT**: I just realized something. The app calls `webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")`. This loads from Android assets. The `index.html` and `assets/` folder should be there.\n\nWith `base: "./"` in vite.config.ts, the HTML should have relative paths like `./assets/index-xxx.js` and the WebView should find them fine.\n\nLet me look at another potential issue: **React StrictMode double-mounting**. In development, StrictMode can cause issues. But in production builds (release APK), StrictMode effects are disabled... actually StrictMode in React is a development tool and has no effect in production.\n\n**Let me look at actual error possibilities more carefully.**\n\nI wonder if the issue is with the `manualChunks: undefined` setting in vite.config.ts. With this, all code is bundled together, potentially creating a very large JS file. On low-end Android devices, parsing a huge JS bundle synchronously might cause OOM or ANR, which appears as a crash.\n\nBUT more importantly - `rollupOptions.output.manualChunks = undefined` in Vite doesn\'t mean "no chunking" - it means "let Rollup decide the default chunking behavior". The default behavior without `manualChunks` still creates multiple chunks for lazy imports.\n\nWait, the comment says:\n```javascript\n// file:// 协议下，动态 import() 跨 chunk 文件在部分 WebView 版本中\n// 受同源策略限制，可能被阻断，导致 React 无法完成初始化渲染。\n// 不拆包后，所有代码合并进少量静态 chunk，WebView 可以顺序加载\n```\n\nSo `manualChunks: undefined` is intentionally preventing manual code splitting. But Vite/Rollup still does automatic code splitting for dynamic imports (`import()`). If the code has any `lazy()` imports (React.lazy), they would still be split into separate chunks.\n\nThis is important! Let me check if the React app uses any lazy loading...\n\nActually, I can check the routes.tsx - it imports all page components directly (no `React.lazy()`), so all pages are bundled together. No dynamic imports = no code splitting issues.\n\nOK, I\'m going around in circles. Let me look at the actual crash from a different angle: what do we know for sure?\n\n1.         fileChooserCallback?.onReceiveValue(uris)

    // ── 下载完成广播 ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    private val downloadReceiver = object : BroadcastReceiver() {
        override fun onReceive(context: Context?, intent: Intent?) {
            Toast.makeText(context, "✓ 文件已下载完成，保存至「下载」文件夹", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()
        }
    }

    // ── JS 桥接口 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    inner class WebAppBridge {

        /** React 首屏就绪后调用，与 3s 最小时间共同触发启动遮罩淡出 */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyReady() {
            webViewReadyReceived = true
            runOnUiThread { tryDismissSplash() }
        }

        /**
         * 主题切换时由 ThemeContext 调用，同步更新原生状态栏与底部导航栏外观。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.notifyTheme(isDark: boolean)
         * @param isDark true = 深色主题，false = 浅色主题
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyTheme(isDark: Boolean) {
            runOnUiThread { applyNativeTheme(isDark) }
        }

        /**
         * 强调色方案切换时由 ThemeContext 调用，同步更新底部导航栏选中图标/文字颜色，
         * 并将 hex 持久化到 SharedPreferences，供下次冷启动时还原到启动画面。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.notifyAccent(primaryHex: string)
         * @param primaryHex 当前方案的主色调 hex 值，如 "#7c3aed"
         */
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyAccent(primaryHex: String) {
            // 持久化 accent hex，供下次冷启动还原到启动画面
            getSharedPreferences("gm_prefs", MODE_PRIVATE)
                .edit().putString("accent_hex", primaryHex).apply()
            runOnUiThread {
                try {
                    val color = Color.parseColor(primaryHex)
                    // 仅更新选中色，未选中色保持不变（取自当前 itemTextColor/iconTintList）
                    val unselected = if (isDarkTheme()) 0xFF9292A8.toInt() else 0xFF64748B.toInt()
                    val iconColors = android.content.res.ColorStateList(
                        arrayOf(intArrayOf(android.R.attr.state_checked), intArrayOf()),
                        intArrayOf(color, unselected)
                    )
                    bottomNav.itemIconTintList = iconColors
                    bottomNav.itemTextColor   = iconColors
                    currentAccentColor = color
                } catch (_: Exception) { /* 非法 hex，静默忽略 */ }
            }
        }

        /**
         * ArtifactsPage 调用：传原始 GitHub URL + token，由原生完成"解析重定向 → 下载"流程。
         *
         * GitHub 所有下载链接（releases/archive/artifacts）均会 302 重定向到
         * S3/CDN 预签名 URL。直接把 Authorization header 转发给预签名 URL 会
         * 触发 S3 签名冲突，导致下载失败。此方法先解析最终 URL 再下载，避免此问题。
         *
         * 调用：window.AndroidBridge.downloadFile(url, fileName, token)
         */
[The command completed with exit code 0.]

    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 冷启动时读取上次保存的主题，默认跟随系统（system 模式）
        val savedTheme = getSharedPreferences("gm_prefs", MODE_PRIVATE)
            .getString("theme_mode", "system") ?: "system"
        val isInitialDark = when (savedTheme) {
            "light" -> false
            "dark"  -> true
            else    -> { // system
                val nightMode = resources.configuration.uiMode and
                    android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_MASK
                nightMode == android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_YES
            }
        }
        // 立即应用与系统/偏好一致的初始颜色，避免深色闪烁
        if (isInitialDark) {
            window.statusBarColor     = Color.parseColor("#111117")
            window.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d0d11")
        } else {
            window.statusBarColor     = Color.parseColor("#f8f8fb")
            window.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#f6f4fa")
            // 浅色模式：状态栏/导航栏图标设为深色
            if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.R) {
                window.insetsController?.setSystemBarsAppearance(
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS or
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS,
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS or
                    android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS
                )
            } else {
                @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
                window.decorView.systemUiVisibility =
                    window.decorView.systemUiVisibility or
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_STATUS_BAR or
                    View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BAR
            }
        }

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)
        bottomNav = findViewById(R.id.bottomNav)

        // 读取上次持久化的主题色，并同步应用到启动画面各元素
        applySavedAccentToSplash()
        // 启动打字动画（与 WebView 加载并行进行）
        startSplashTypingAnimation()

        // ── WebView 预加载优化 ───────────────────────────────────────
        // 先完成所有 WebView 配置，再尽早调用 loadUrl，
        // 确保 JS bundle 解析可以在启动画面展示的 3s 内完成。
        setupWebViewSettings()
        setupWebViewClient()
        setupWebChromeClient()
        setupDownloadListener()
        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")

        // WebView 最早时机开始加载，充分利用 3s 启动时间预热 React
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }

        registerDownloadReceiver()
        setupBottomNav()

        // 3s 最小展示时间到达后更新门禁状态，与 notifyReady 共同决定是否消除启动画面
        splashHandler.postDelayed({
            splashMinTimeReached = true
            tryDismissSplash()
        }, 3000L)

        // 6s 硬兜底：防止 notifyReady 永不触发（如 JS 崩溃）时启动画面卡死
        splashHandler.postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 6000L)
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    override fun onDestroy() {
        super.onDestroy()
        splashHandler.removeCallbacksAndMessages(null)
        unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)
        webView.stopLoading()
        webView.destroy()
    }

<action>
AgentThinkAction(thought='\nNow I have a much clearer picture. Let me analyze the potential crash causes:\n\n**Critical Issue Found**: In `onCreate()`, `darkTheme` is still set to `true` (default) when `setupWebViewSettings()` is called, even though `isInitialDark` correctly detects the actual dark mode. The `darkTheme` variable is never updated with `isInitialDark`. This means in light mode, the WebView gets a dark background.\n\nBut more importantly, this is not the CRASH cause. Let me look for actual crashes.\n\n**Issue 1 - `onDestroy()` unregisters without checking**: \n```kotlin\noverride fun onDestroy() {\n    super.onDestroy()\n    splashHandler.removeCallbacksAndMessages(null)\n    unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)  // CRASH if not registered\n    webView.stopLoading()\n    webView.destroy()\n}\n```\nIf anything crashes before `registerDownloadReceiver()` in `onCreate()`, the `onDestroy()` call would crash with `IllegalArgumentException: Receiver not registered`.\n\n**Issue 2 - `window.statusBarColor` and `window.navigationBarColor` called BEFORE `setContentView()`**:\nLooking at `onCreate()`:\n```kotlin\noverride fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {\n    super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)\n    // ...\n    window.statusBarColor = ...  // Called BEFORE setContentView\n    window.navigationBarColor = ...  // Called BEFORE setContentView\n    // ...\n    setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)  // Called AFTER window manipulations\n```\n\n`window.statusBarColor` and `window.navigationBarColor` are valid to call before `setContentView()`. This is actually a common pattern.\n\n**Issue 3 - The REAL crash I think**: Let me look at `setupWebViewSettings()` again:\n```kotlin\nprivate fun setupWebViewSettings() {\n    val bgHex = if (darkTheme) "#111117" else "#f8f8fb"\n    webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor(bgHex))\n```\n\n`darkTheme = true` by default, so this always uses dark theme initially. But `isInitialDark` is correctly calculated. The bug is that `darkTheme` is never set from `isInitialDark`. But again - this is a visual bug, not a crash.\n\n**The ACTUAL CRASH**: Looking at the `window.decorView.systemUiVisibility` call on API < 30 (before `APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS` was introduced):\n\n```kotlin\n} else {\n    @Suppress("DEPRECATION")\n    window.decorView.systemUiVisibility =\n        window.decorView.systemUiVisibility or\n        View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_STATUS_BAR or\n        View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BAR\n}\n```\n\n`View.SYSTEM_UI_FLAG_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BAR` was added in API 26 (minSdk=26), so this should be fine.\n`Build.VERSION_CODES.R` = API 30.\n\nSo on API 26-29, the `else` branch runs. `window.decorView.systemUiVisibility` is deprecated but shouldn\'t crash.\n\n**FOUND IT - The Real Crash**: \n\nLooking at `window.insetsController?.setSystemBarsAppearance(...)` with `APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS`:\n- `APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS` is defined as `android.view.WindowInsetsController.APPEARANCE_LIGHT_STATUS_BARS`\n- This is available from API 30 (Android 11)\n- The code checks `Build.VERSION_CODES.R` (= API 30) ✓\n\nThis is fine.\n\nWait, let me look at something else. Looking at `android.content.res.Configuration.UI_MODE_NIGHT_MASK` - this constant has always existed. Fine.\n\nLet me look at a potentially fatal crash:\n\n**CRITICAL FINDING**: `APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS` was added in API 30 but requires **windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode** AND the navigation bar must not be gesture-based. But on Android 10+ with gesture navigation, `APPEARANCE_LIGHT_NAVIGATION_BARS` might not have effect anyway.\n\nBut this still shouldn\'t crash.\n\n**THE CRASH - Most likely**: \nI think the crash is from the `windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode` attribute:\n```xml\n<item name="android:windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode">shortEdges</item>\n```\n\nOn Android 8 (API 26-27), `windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode` doesn\'t exist. But the system should ignore unknown style attributes gracefully. \n\nActually wait - `windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode` was added in API 28. On API 26-27, the theme attribute `android:windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode` is unknown. The Android resource system will simply skip unknown attributes, NOT crash.\n\n**Hmm... Let me think about what REALLY causes the crash on GitHub-built APKs specifically.**\n\nThe key point is: "GitHub构建的安卓APP启动时会立即闪退". But what about the `BottomNavigationView` and its associated classes?\n\nActually, `com.google.android.material:material:1.12.0` should include its own ProGuard consumer rules. These are embedded in the AAR and automatically applied.\n\n**BUT**: What if `isShrinkResources = true` removes a needed drawable or layout? Let me think... `shrinkResources` removes unused resources, but the system considers all referenced resources as "used". If a drawable is only referenced from code (not XML), it might be removed!\n\nActually in this case:\n- `ic_nav_ai.xml` - referenced from XML menu\n- `ic_launcher.xml` - referenced from manifest\n- etc.\n\nThese are all properly referenced from XML, so `shrinkResources` shouldn\'t remove them.\n\n**FINAL ANALYSIS**: I believe the primary crash cause is:\n\n1. **`darkTheme` not synchronized with `isInitialDark`**: Minor visual issue.\n\n2. **`unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)` in `onDestroy()` without checking**: If any initialization error occurs before `registerDownloadReceiver()` is called, this will cause a secondary crash when the Activity is destroyed. BUT what\'s the PRIMARY crash?\n\n3. **The PRIMARY crash**: I think it might be in `setupWebViewSettings()` calling deprecated APIs that don\'t exist on certain API levels or certain Android vendors (like Huawei, Samsung) that customize WebView behavior.\n\nOR, more likely - the issue is with ProGuard stripping something important. The `proguard-rules.pro` only explicitly keeps `WebAppBridge` and some appcompat classes. What about other important classes?\n\nActually, reading more carefully: `appcompat:1.7.0` includes consumer ProGuard rules. `material:1.12.0` includes consumer ProGuard rules. `activity-ktx:1.9.3` includes consumer ProGuard rules.\n\nSo the built-in rules from these libraries should cover everything...\n\n**WAIT - I just found a REAL issue**: \n\nLooking at `onDestroy()`:\n```kotlin\noverride fun onDestroy() {\n    super.onDestroy()\n    splashHandler.removeCallbacksAndMessages(null)\n    unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)\n    webView.stopLoading()\n    webView.destroy()\n}\n```\n\nIf `onCreate()` crashes early (before `registerDownloadReceiver()` and `webView` initialization), then when Android calls `onDestroy()`:\n1. `unregisterReceiver(downloadReceiver)` → `IllegalArgumentException`\n2. `webView.stopLoading()` → `NullPointerException` (webView is lateinit, not initialized)\n3. `webView.destroy()` → `NullPointerException`\n\nThis cascading crash makes it look like the app "crashes immediately" when in fact there might be a different root cause in `onCreate()`.\n\nSo I need to:\n1. The style `BottomNavTextActive` uses `android:fontFamily="sans-serif-medium"`. If the theme parent was wrong, the app would crash at `setContentView()` when inflating the layout that uses Material components. The error would be:\n```\nIllegalArgumentException: The style on this component requires your app theme to be Theme.MaterialComponents\n```\n\nBut we\'re using `Theme.MaterialComponents.Light.NoActionBar` which IS a MaterialComponents theme! So Material3 components would fail if used with a MaterialComponents theme... but we\'re using `BottomNavigationView` which is a Material2 component.\n\nOR wait - with material 1.12.0, is `BottomNavigationView` still a Material2 component or is it Material3? I believe in 1.12.0, `BottomNavigationView` is the Material2 bottom navigation. The Material3 equivalent is `NavigationBarView`/`BottomNavigationView` (same class actually, but the styling behavior differs).\n\nWith material 1.12.0 and `Theme.MaterialComponents`:\n- Some Material3-specific attributes might not be defined in the MaterialComponents theme\n- This could cause `InflateException` when trying to inflate `BottomNavigationView` which tries to read Material3 attributes from the theme\n\nThis IS a known issue! Starting from material 1.5.0, `BottomNavigationView` started using some M3 attributes like `colorSurface`, `colorSurfaceVariant`, etc. These attributes exist in both M2 and M3 themes, BUT their default values differ.\n\nActually, I don\'t think this would crash the app either, because the MaterialComponents theme defines all the necessary attributes.\n\n**FINAL CONCLUSION**: \n\nBased on all my analysis, I believe there are multiple issues that together cause the crash:\n\n1. **Primary crash cause**: The `onDestroy()` unregisters `downloadReceiver` without checking if it was registered. While this should work, on some MIUI/EMUI/OneUI variants, calling window methods before `setContentView()` can cause crashes.\n\nActually, I just noticed: `window.statusBarColor` requires that the theme has `android:windowDrawsSystemBarBackgrounds = true` (or the theme requires the window to draw system bar backgrounds).     // ── 广播 ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    private fun registerDownloadReceiver() {
        val filter = IntentFilter(DownloadManager.ACTION_DOWNLOAD_COMPLETE)
        if (Build.VERSION.SDK_INT >= Build.VERSION_CODES.TIRAMISU) {
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter, Context.RECEIVER_NOT_EXPORTED)
        } else {
            @Suppress("UnspecifiedRegisterReceiverFlag")
            registerReceiver(downloadReceiver, filter)
        }
    }
}
